After the appraisal, I found that (1) the Zen room is similar to a modern apar**ent, and it can satisfy people who are not very picky about the accommodation environment. After all, the indoor area is large, there are balconies and sofas, and the price is relatively relatively Friendly, just a few households in one elevator, it seems simple. (2) The first half of the picture is the thatched hut in Yunshuijian. The environment of this area is the most distinctive, so there are many tourists who come to check in outside the hotel. Tourists cannot enter the hotel. After entering the inner area of the hotel, it is relatively quiet. Each room is a detached courtyard. In addition to the small size of the interior, there is a front yard and a backyard, and the interior decoration is also quite good, which is similar to the experience of Banyan Tree in Anji (but the breakfast is relatively simple per person, and the choice Little but enough to eat) People who have requirements for the quality of accommodation and care about privacy and tranquility can choose Yunshuijian Inn. (3) The ordinary house in the picture is a Japanese-style room type. After entering the ordinary house compound, there is also a large area inside, which is very elegant and quiet. Each room should have a small courtyard of different sizes, but The interior decoration and beds are all Japanese style. People who like quietness and tatami beds can choose the room type in this area, because they are all on the first floor, and it is very comfortable to make a pot of tea with the courtyard door open. Each type of room has a different style. There are different butlers in different areas (the areas can be reached within walking distance if luggage is easy to carry). The butler service is very good. Yunshuijian seems to be relatively high-grade. There are two butlers and restaurants In the park, the experience will be better. The evening performances are the most eye-catching part of Nianhua Bay, and the quality of the performances is also very good. Basically, you come here to watch the watch Acting, eating and drinking. The disadvantage is that the entire scenic spot is too crowded and noisy during the day and before the performance at night. Only after the performance is over can the hotel area return to quietness. In addition, the rooms are basically not big. The advantage is that the performance is very beautiful, and the inn and hotel also have their own characteristics.
